   lakucādyantarvyājaṃ tathā bahirvyājamatra mocādi /	lakuca-Adi-antar-vyAjam taTA bahis-vyAjam-atra mocA-Adi /
   āmrādyubhayavyājaṃ sarvavyājaṃ ca kakubhādi //	Amra-Adi-uBaya-vyAjam sarva-vyAjam ca kakuBa-Adi //
   panasādi bahuvyājaṃ nīlakapitthādi bhavati nirvyājam /	panasa-Adi bahu-vyAjam nIla-kapitTa-Adi Bavati nirvyAjam /
   sakalaphalānāṃ ṣoḍhā jñātavyaḥ kavibhiriti bhedaḥ //	sakala-PalAnAm zoXA jQAtavyaH kaviBiH-iti BedaH //
   ekadvitryādibhedena sāmastyenāthavā ṛtūn /	eka-dvi-tri-Adi-Bedena sAmastyena-aTavA RtUn /
   prabandheṣu nibandhīyātkrameṇa vyutkrameṇa vā //	prabanDezu nibanDIyAt-krameNa vyutkrameNa vA //
   na ca vyutkramadoṣo 'sti kaverarthapathaspṛśaḥ /	na ca vyutkrama-dozaH asti kaveH-arTa-paTa-spRSaH /
   tathā tathā kāpi bhaved vyutkramo bhūṣāṇāṃ yathā //	taTA taTA kA-api Bavet vyutkramaH BUzANAm yaTA //
   anusandhānaśūnyasya bhūṣaṇaṃ dūṣaṇāyate /	anusanDAna-SUnyasya BUzaNam dUzaNAyate /
   sāvadhānasya ca kaverdūṣaṇaṃ bhūṣaṇāyate //	sa-avaDAnasya ca kaveH-dUzaNam BUzaNAyate //
   iti kālavibhāgasya darśitā vṛttirīdṛśī /	iti kAla-viBAgasya darSitA vRttiH-IdRSI /
   kaveriha mahānmoha iha siddho mahākaviḥ //	kaveH-iha mahAn-mohaH iha sidDaH mahA-kaviH //
   iti rājaśekharakṛtau kāvyamīmāṃsāyāṃ kavirahasye prathame 'dhikaraṇe	iti rAja-SeKara-kRtO kAvya-mImAMsAyAm kavi-rahasye praTame aDikaraNe
   kālavibhāgo nāma aṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ	kAlaviBAgaH nAma azwAdaSaH aDyAyaH
   samātpamidaṃ prathamamadhikaraṇaṃ kavirahasyaṃ kāvyamīmāṃsāyām	samAtpam-idam praTamam-aDikaraNam kavi-rahasyam kAvya-mImAMsAyAm
